# Text Elements
On a hot summer day, 25 bags of ice (5kg each) at -60c are added to a swimming pool at 30.0c. 
The water in the swimming pool has a mass of 10000.0kg. calculate the final temperatures of the pool water.  ^bfuOyBMC

mass of pool ^useUAlnp
